<p><b>Sebastião Barroso Lazaroni</b>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-enciclopediaselecao_1-0"><a href="#cite_note-enciclopediaselecao-1">[1]</a></sup> commonly known as <b>Sebastião Lazaroni</b> (born September 25, 1950<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-enciclopediaselecao_1-1"><a href="#cite_note-enciclopediaselecao-1">[1]</a></sup>), is a <a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazilian</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Football_(soccer)" title="Football (soccer)">football (soccer)</a> manager who last coached <a href="/wiki/Qatar_Stars_League" title="Qatar Stars League">Qatar Stars League</a> club <a href="/wiki/Qatar_SC" title="Qatar SC">Qatar SC</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Third_spell_at_Qatar_SC_2-0"><a href="#cite_note-Third_spell_at_Qatar_SC-2">[2]</a></sup> He was born in <a href="/wiki/Muria%C3%A9" title="Muriaé">Muriaé</a>, <a href="/wiki/Minas_Gerais" title="Minas Gerais">Minas Gerais state</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-enciclopediaselecao_1-2"><a href="#cite_note-enciclopediaselecao-1">[1]</a></sup></p>
<p>He is well known in Brazil as the manager who tried to introduce the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Libero_(football)" title="Libero (football)">libero</a> position in Brazilian football.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-enciclopedialance_3-0"><a href="#cite_note-enciclopedialance-3">[3]</a></sup> He used the <a href="/wiki/Formation_(association_football)#3.E2.80.935.E2.80.932" title="Formation (association football)">3-5-2</a> scheme during the <a href="/wiki/1990_FIFA_World_Cup" title="1990 FIFA World Cup">1990 FIFA World Cup</a>, but it was a failure, and <a href="/wiki/Brazil_national_football_team" title="Brazil national football team">Brazil</a> was eliminated in the second round by <a href="/wiki/Argentina_national_football_team" title="Argentina national football team">Argentina</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-enciclopedialance_3-1"><a href="#cite_note-enciclopedialance-3">[3]</a></sup></p>
<p>When he was the <a href="/wiki/Brazil_national_football_team" title="Brazil national football team">Brazil national team</a> head coach, in 35 matches, he won 21, drew seven and lost seven.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-enciclopedialance_3-2"><a href="#cite_note-enciclopedialance-3">[3]</a></sup></p>
<p>Champion of South America Cup after 39 years of fasting in 1989</p>
<p>He is also known for his being the head coach of Turkish club <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Fenerbah%C3%A7e_SK" title="Fenerbahçe SK">Fenerbahçe</a> that ended the 40-year undefeated European home record of Manchester United in the European Champions' League match in 1996.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-4"><a href="#cite_note-4">[4]</a></sup></p>
<p>He took over the Qatar national team on August 1, 2011 as a replacement for <a href="/wiki/Milovan_Rajevac" title="Milovan Rajevac">Milovan Rajevac</a>, but was ultimately fired four months later as a result of the team's unimpressive performances. The <a href="/wiki/Qatar_Football_Association" title="Qatar Football Association">QFA</a> highlighted his failure to advance past the group stage of the <a href="/wiki/2011_Pan_Arab_Games" title="2011 Pan Arab Games">2011 Pan Arab Games</a>, which Qatar had hosted, as a main cause of his sacking. His record with the team ended with two wins, five draws and two losses.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-qfasacked_5-0"><a href="#cite_note-qfasacked-5">[5]</a></sup> He was officially sacked on January 3, 2012 after his contract was released by QFA.</p>
<p>Lazaroni was last in charge of <a href="/wiki/Qatar_SC" title="Qatar SC">Qatar SC</a> for the third time in his career following spells with the <a href="/wiki/Doha" title="Doha">Doha</a> based club between 2008–2011 and 2012–2014.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Third_spell_at_Qatar_SC_2-1"><a href="#cite_note-Third_spell_at_Qatar_SC-2">[2]</a></sup> His third spell ended in disappointment and he was dismissed in May 2016 after the club's relegation from <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_Qatar_Stars_League" title="2015–16 Qatar Stars League">Qatar Stars League</a>.</p>
<p></p>
